How many trick or treaters did you have Halloween night?: 25-50
Timestamp: 11/1/2017 9:54:42
Where do you live?: 5900 Larch St
What kind of candy were you handing out?: Mini chocolate bars + cans of pop
How decorated is your house?: Couple of Jack O'Lanterns
Comments: Kids mostly came in big groups, as if one parent was shepherding around a big collective. All kids were very polite - like when we asked what candy they wanted, they would say "Anything is fine!" Costumes were pretty low-effort, lots of little firemen or paramedics (wearing regular jackets with stickers or patches). A couple of teens came by-- the house is by a park, so they took a break from shooting firecrackers (an eternal teen Halloween tradition!). We handed out candy at my parents' house in Kerrisdale, where I used to trick or treat as a kid (I'm 30 now). To me it appears there are way fewer kids, which I think is borne out by the data, but still - it's kind of wild when I remember the huge crowds of kids on the sidewalks in my youth vs the sparse little clusters we saw last night.
Optional: Your email address:
Location: 36.2048072,-86.7246222
